    WHERE NOT (e."IsDeleted")
    ORDER BY e."CreatedAt" DESC
    LIMIT @__p_1 OFFSET @__p_0
) AS e0
INNER JOIN "Users" AS u ON e0."OrganizerId" = u."Id"
ORDER BY e0."CreatedAt" DESC
